   Śatasāhasrikā Prajñaparamitā	Śata sAhasrikA PrajQa paramitA
   (ŚsP_II 1_1)	(ŚsP_II 1_1)
   oṃ namaḥ sarvabuddhabodhisattvebhyaḥ.	om namaH sarva budDa boDisattveByaH.
   pṛthivīdhātvasattayāyuṣmañ chāradvatīputra pūrvāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	pRTivI DAtu asat tayA Ayuzman CAradvatI putra pUrva antataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   pṛthivīdhātuśūnyatayā pūrvāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	pRTivI DAtu SUnya tayA pUrva antataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   pṛthivīdhātuviviktatayā pūrvāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	pRTivI DAtu vivikta tayA pUrva antataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   pṛthivīdhātvasvabhāvatayā pūrvāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	pRTivI DAtu asvaBAva tayA pUrva antataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   pṛthivīdhātvasattayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	pRTivI DAtvasat tayA parAntataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   pṛthivīdhātuśūnyatayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	pRTivI DAtu SUnya tayA apara antataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   pṛthivīdhātuviviktatayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	pRTivI DAtu vivikta tayA apara antataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   pṛthivīdhātvasvabhāvatayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	pRTivI DAtu asva BAva tayA parAntataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   pṛthivīdhātvasattayā madhyato bodhisattvo nopaiti, pṛthivīdhātuśūnyatayā	pRTivI DAtvasat tayA maDyatas boDisattvaH na upEti, pRTivI DAtu SUnya tayA
   madhyato bodhisattvo nopaiti, pṛthivīdhātuviviktatayā madhyato bodhisattvo	maDyataH boDisattvaH na upEti, pRTivI DAtu vivikta tayA maDyatas boDisattvaH 
   nopaiti, pṛthivīdhātvasvabhāvatayā madhyato bodhisattvo nopaiti. tat kasya	na upEti, pRTivI DAtu asvaBAva tayA maDyatas boDisattvaH na upEti. tat kasya
   hetoḥ? na hy āyuṣmañ chāradvatīputra pṛthivīdhātvasattāyāṃ	hetoH? na hi Ayuzman CAradvatI putra pRTivI DAtu asattAyAm
   pṛthivīdhātuśūnyatāyāṃ pṛthivīdhātuviviktatāyāṃ pṛthivīdhātvasvabhāvatāyāṃ	pRTivI DAtu SUnyatAyAm pRTivI DAtu vivikta tAyAm pRTivI DAtu asva BAva tAyAm
   pūrvānta upalabhyate nāparānta upalabhyate na madhyam upalabhyate. na	pUrva ante upalaByate na aparAntaH upalaByate na maDyam upalaByate. na
   cānyā pṛthivīdhātvasattānyā pṛthivīdhātuśūnyatānyā	ca anyA pRTivI DAtu asattA anyA pRTivI DAtu SUnyatA anyA
   pṛthivīdhātuviviktatānyā pṛthivīdhātvasvabhāvatānyo bodhisattvo 'nyaḥ	pRTivI DAtu vivikta tA anyA pRTivI DAtu asva BAva tA anyaH boDisattvaH anyaH
   pūrvānto 'nyo 'parānto 'nyan madhyam iti hy āyuṣmañ chāradvatīputra yā ca	pUrva antaH anyaH apara antaH anyat maDyam iti hi Ayuzman CAradvatI putra yA ca
   pṛthivīdhātvasattā yā ca pṛthivīdhātuśūnyatā yā ca pṛthivīdhātuviviktatā	pRTivI DAtvasattA yA ca pRTivI DAtu SUnyatA yA ca pRTivI DAtu vivikta tA
   yā ca pṛthivīdhātvasvabhāvatā yaś ca bodhisattvo yaś ca pūrvānto yaś	yA ca pRTivI DAtu asvaBAva tA yaH ca boDisattvaH yaH ca pUrva antaH yaH 
   cāparānto yac ca madhyaṃ sarvam etad advayam advaidhīkāram.	ca aparAntaH yat ca maDyam sarvam etat advayam advEDIkAram.
   abdhātvasattayāyuṣmañ chāradvatīputra pūrvāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti.	abDAtu asat tayA Ayuzman CAradvatI putra pUrva antataH boDisattvaH na upEti.
   abdhātuśūnyatayā pūrvāntano bodhisattvo nopaiti, abdhātuviviktatayā	ap DAtu SUnya tayA pUrva antanaH boDisattvaH na upEti, ap DAtu vivikta tayA
   pūrvāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti, abdhātvasvabhāvatayā pūrvāntato	pUrva antataH boDisattvaH na upEti, abDAtu asvaBAva tayA pUrva antataH 
   bodhisattvo nopaiti, abdhātvasattayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	boDisattvaH na upEti, abDAtu asat tayA parAntataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   abdhātuśūnyatayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti, abdhātuviviktatayāparāntato	ap DAtu SUnya tayA apara antataH boDisattvaH na upEti, ap DAtu vivikta tayA aparAntato
   bodhisattvo nopaiti, abdhātvasvabhāvatayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	boDisattvaH na upEti, abDAtu asvaBAva tayA parAntataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   abdhātvasattayā madhyato bodhisattvo nopaiti, abdhātuśūnyatayā madhyato	abDAtu asat tayA maDyatas boDisattvaH na upEti, abDAtu SUnyatayA maDyatas 
   (ŚsP_II 1_2) bodhisattvo nopaiti, abdhātuviviktatayā madhyato bodhisattvo	(ŚsP_II 1_2) boDisattvaH na upEti, ap DAtu vivikta tayA maDyatas boDisattvaH 
   nopaiti, abdhātvasvabhāvatayā madhyato bodhisattvo nopaiti. tat kasya	na upEti, abDAtu asvaBAva tayA maDyatas boDisattvaH na upEti. tat kasya
   hetoḥ? na hy āyuṣmañ chāradvatīputrābdhātvasattāyām abdhātuśūnyatāyām	hetoH? na hi Ayuzman CAradvatI putra abDAtva sattAyAm ap DAtu SUnyatAyAm
   abdhātuviviktatāyām abdhātvasvabhāvatāyāṃ pūrvānta upalabhyate nāparānta	ap DAtu vivikta tAyAm abDAtu asvaBAvatAyAm pUrva ante upalaByate na aparAnta
   upalabhyate na madhyam upalabhyate. na	upalaByate na maDyam upalaByate. na
   cānyābdhātvasattānyābdhātuśūnyatānyābdhātuviviktatānyābdhātvasvabhāvatānyo	ca anyAbDAtu a sattAnyAp DAtu SUnya tAnyAp DAtu vivikta tAnyAbDAtva svaBAva tA anyaH 
   bodhisattvo 'nyaḥ pūrvānto 'nyo 'parānto 'nyan madhyam iti hy āyuṣmañ	boDisattvaH anyaH pUrva antaH anyaH apara antaH anyat maDyam iti hi Ayuzman 
   chāradvatīputra yā cābdhātvasattā yā cābdhātuśūnyatā yā cābdhātuviviktatā	CAradvatI putra yA ca abDAtu asat tA yA ca abDAtu SUnyatA yA ca abDAtu vivikta tA
   yā cābdhātvasvabhāvatā yaś ca bodhisattvo yaś ca pūrvānto yaś cāparānto	yA ca abDAtu asvaBAva tA yaH ca boDisattvaH yaH ca pUrva antaH yaH ca aparAntaH 
   yac ca madhyaṃ sarvam etad advayam advaidhīkāram.	yat ca maDyam sarvam etat advayam advEDIkAram.
   tejodhātvasattayāyuṣmañ chāradvatīputra pūrvāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	tejaH DAtu asat tayA Ayuzman CAradvatI putra pUrva antataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   tejodhātuśūnyatayā pūrvāntano bodhisattvo nopaiti, tejodhātuviviktatayā	tejaH DAtu SUnya tayA pUrva antanaH boDisattvaH na upEti, tejaH DAtu vivikta tayA
   pūrvāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti, tejodhātvasvabhāvatayā pūrvāntato	pUrva antataH boDisattvaH na upEti, tejaH DAtu asvaBAva tayA pUrva antataH 
   bodhisattvo nopaiti, tejodhātvasattayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	boDisattvaH na upEti, tejaH DAtu a sat tayA parAntataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   tejodhātvuśūnyatayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	tejaH DAtvu SUnya tayA aparAntataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   tejodhātuviviktatayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	tejaH DAtu vivikta tayA apara antataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   tejodhātvasvabhāvatayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti, tejodhātvasattayā	tejaH DAtu asvaBAva tayA parAntataH boDisattvaH na upEti, tejaH DAtu a sat tayA
   madhyato bodhisattvo nopaiti, tejodhātuśūnyatayā madhyato bodhisattvo	maDyataH boDisattvaH na upEti, tejaH DAtu SUnya tayA maDyatas boDisattvaH 
   nopaiti, tejodhātuviviktatayā madhyato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	na upEti, tejaH DAtu vivikta tayA maDyatas boDisattvaH na upEti,
   tejodhātvasvabhāvatayā madhyato bodhisattvo nopaiti. tat kasya hetoḥ? na	tejaH DAtu asvaBAva tayA maDyatas boDisattvaH na upEti. tat kasya hetoH? na
   hy āyuṣmañ chāradvatīputra tejodhātvasattāyāṃ tejodhātuśūnyatāyāṃ	hi Ayuzman CAradvatI putra tejaH DAtu a sattAyAm tejaH DAtu SUnyatAyAm
   tejodhātuviviktatāyāṃ tejodhātvasvabhāvatāyāṃ pūrvānta upalabhyate	tejaH DAtu vivikta tAyAm tejaH DAtu asvaBAvatAyAm pUrva ante upalaByate
   nāparānta upalabhyate na madhyam upalabhyate. na cānyā tejodhātvasattānyā	na aparAntaH upalaByate na maDyam upalaByate. na ca anyA tejaH DAtu a sattA anyA
   tejodhātuśūnyatānyā tejodhātuviviktatānyā tejodhātvasvabhāvatānyo	tejaH DAtu SUnyatA anyA tejaH DAtu vivikta tA anyA tejaH DAtu asvaBAva tA anyaH 
   bodhisattvo 'nyaḥ pūrvānto 'nyo 'parānto 'nyan madhyam iti hy āyuṣmañ	boDisattvaH anyaH pUrva antaH anyaH apara antaH anyat maDyam iti hi Ayuzman 
   chāradvatīputra yā ca tejodhātvasattā yā ca tejodhātuśūnyatā yā ca	CAradvatI putra yA ca tejaH DAtu a sattA yA ca tejaH DAtu SUnyatA yA ca
   tejodhātuviviktatā yā ca tejodhātvasvabhāvatā yaś ca bodhisattvo yaś ca	tejaH DAtu vivikta tA yA ca tejaH DAtu asvaBAva tA yaH ca boDisattvaH yaH ca
   pūrvānto yaś cāparānto yac ca madhyaṃ sarvam etad advayam advaidhīkāram.	pUrva antaH yaH ca aparAntaH yat ca maDyam sarvam etat advayam advEDIkAram.
   vāyudhātvasattayāyuṣmañ chāradvatīputra pūrvāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	vAyuDAtu asattayA Ayuzman CAradvatI putra pUrva antataH boDisattvaH na upEti,

   pūrvāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti, vāyudhātvasvabhāvatayā pūrvāntato	pUrva antataH boDisattvaH na upEti, vAyuDAtu asvaBAva tayA pUrva antataH 
   bodhisattvo nopaiti, vāyudhātvasattayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	boDisattvaH na upEti, vAyuDAtu asat tayA parAntataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   vāyudhātvuśūnyatayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	vAyuDAtu u SUnya tayA aparAntataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   vāyudhātuviviktatayāparāntato bodhisattvo nopaiti,	vAyu DAtu vivikta tayA apara antataH boDisattvaH na upEti,
   vāyudhātvasvabhāvatayāparāntato (ŚsP_II 1_3) bodhisattvo nopaiti,	vAyuDAtu asvaBAva tayA parAntataH (ŚsP_II 1_3) boDisattvaH na upEti,
   vāyudhātvasattayā madhyato bodhisattvo nopaiti, vāyudhātuśūnyatayā	vAyuDAtu asat tayA maDyatas boDisattvaH na upEti, vAyu DAtu SUnya tayA
   madhyato bodhisattvo nopaiti, vāyudhātuviviktatayā madhyato bodhisattvo	maDyataH boDisattvaH na upEti, vAyu DAtu vivikta tayA maDyatas boDisattvaH

   hetoḥ? na hy āyuṣmañ chāradvatīputra vāyudhātvasattāyāṃ	hetoH? na hi Ayuzman CAradvatI putra vAyuDAtu asattAyAm
   vāyudhātuśūnyatāyāṃ vāyudhātuviviktatāyāṃ vāyudhātvasvabhāvatāyāṃ pūrvānta	vAyu DAtu SUnyatAyAm vAyu DAtu viviktatAyAm vAyuDAtu asvaBAvatAyAm pUrva anta
   upalabhyate nāparānta upalabhyate na madhyam upalabhyate. na cānyā	upalaByate na aparAntaH upalaByate na maDyam upalaByate. na ca anyA
   vāyudhātvasattānyā vāyudhātuśūnyatānyā vāyudhātuviviktatānyā	vAyuDAtu asattA anyA vAyu DAtu SUnyatA anyA vAyu DAtu vivikta tA anyA

   madhyam iti hy āyuṣmañ chāradvatīputra yā ca vāyudhātvasattā yā ca	maDyam iti hi Ayuzman CAradvatI putra yA ca vAyuDAtu asattA yA ca
   vāyudhātuśūnyatā yā ca vāyudhātuviviktatā yā ca vāyudhātvasvabhāvatā yaś	vAyu DAtu SUnyatA yA ca vAyu DAtu vivikta tA yA ca vAyuDAtu asvaBAva tA yaH 
   ca bodhisattvo yaś ca pūrvānto yaś cāparānto yac ca madhyaṃ sarvam etad	ca boDisattvaH yaH ca pUrva antaH yaH ca aparAntaH yat ca maDyam sarvam etat 
   advayam advaidhīkāram.	advayam advEDIkAram.

   ākāśadhātuśūnyatayā pūrvāntano bodhisattvo nopaiti, ākāśadhātuviviktatayā	AkASa DAtu SUnya tayA pUrva antanaH boDisattvaH na upEti, AkASa DAtu vivikta tayA
